      <section class="u-mb-48 u-mt-24" data-track-component="search grid" id="search-article-list">
       <div class="u-container">
        <ul class="app-article-list-row">
         <li class="app-article-list-row__item">
          <div class="u-full-height">
           <div class="u-full-height" data-native-ad-placement="false">
            <article class="u-full-height c-card c-card--flush" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ScholarlyArticle">
             <div class="c-card__layout u-full-height">
              <div class="c-card__image">
               <picture>
                <source sizes="
                                    (max-width: 640px) 160px,
                                    (max-width: 1200px) 290px,
                                    290px" srcset="
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w165h90/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-025-57430-4/MediaObjects/41467_2025_57430_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 160w,
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-025-57430-4/MediaObjects/41467_2025_57430_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 290w" type="image/webp">
                 <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-025-57430-4/MediaObjects/41467_2025_57430_Fig1_HTML.png"/>
                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41467-025-57430-4" itemprop="url">
                 DrBioRight 2.0: an LLM-powered bioinformatics chatbot for large-scale cancer functional proteomics analysis
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Functional proteomics enhances cancer research by identifying biomarkers and therapeutic targets. Here, the authors develop a cancer functional proteomics resource and introduce a resource using reverse phase protein arrays and antibodies targeting key pathways. To improve accessibility, they introduce DrBioRight, an AI-powered platform for intuitive data analysis and visualization.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Wei Liu
                 </span>
                </li>
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Jun Li
                 </span>
                </li>
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Han Liang
                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="c-card__section c-meta">
              <span class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="article.type">
               <span class="c-meta__type">
                Research
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="open-access" itemprop="openAccess">
               <span class="u-color-open-access">
                Open Access
               </span>
              </span>
              <time class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" datetime="2025-03-06" itemprop="datePublished">
               06 Mar 2025
              </time>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg u-text-bold" data-test="journal-title-and-link">
               Nature Communications
              </div>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="volume-and-page-info">
               Volume: 16, P: 1-6
              </div>
             </div>
            </article>
           </div>
          </div>
         </li>
         <li class="app-article-list-row__item">
          <div class="u-full-height">
           <div class="u-full-height" data-native-ad-placement="false">
            <article class="u-full-height c-card c-card--flush" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ScholarlyArticle">
             <div class="c-card__layout u-full-height">
              <div class="c-card__image">
               <picture>
                <source sizes="
                                    (max-width: 640px) 160px,
                                    (max-width: 1200px) 290px,
                                    290px" srcset="
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w165h90/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-025-57426-0/MediaObjects/41467_2025_57426_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 160w,
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-025-57426-0/MediaObjects/41467_2025_57426_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 290w" type="image/webp">
                 <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-025-57426-0/MediaObjects/41467_2025_57426_Fig1_HTML.png"/>
                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41467-025-57426-0" itemprop="url">
                 Towards a holistic framework for multimodal LLM in 3D brain CT radiology report generation
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) hold promise for a range of medical applications. Here, the authors use MLLMs for 3D brain CT radiology report generation, demonstrating that combining anatomy-aware model fine-tuning with robust evaluation metrics establishes a comprehensive and effective framework.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Cheng-Yi Li
                 </span>
                </li>
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Kao-Jung Chang
                 </span>
                </li>
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Shih-Hwa Chiou
                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="c-card__section c-meta">
              <span class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="article.type">
               <span class="c-meta__type">
                Research

                </source>
               </picture>

              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41591-024-03425-5" itemprop="url">
                 The TRIPOD-LLM reporting guideline for studies using large language models
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 TRIPOD-LLM (transparent reporting of a multivariable model for individual prognosis or diagnosis–large language model) is a checklist of items considered essential for good reporting of studies that are developing or evaluating an LLM for use in healthcare settings. It is a ‘living guideline’ that emphasizes transparency, human oversight and task-specific performance reporting.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">

                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>

                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s42256-024-00976-7" itemprop="url">
                 What large language models know and what people think they know
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Understanding how people perceive and interpret uncertainty from large language models (LLMs) is crucial, as users often overestimate LLM accuracy, especially with default explanations. Steyvers et al. show that aligning LLM explanations with their internal confidence improves user perception.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

                 </span>
                </li>

                 </span>
                </li>

            <article class="u-full-height c-card c-card--flush" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ScholarlyArticle">
             <div class="c-card__layout u-full-height">
              <div class="c-card__image">
               <picture>
                <source sizes="
                                    (max-width: 640px) 160px,
                                    (max-width: 1200px) 290px,
                                    290px" srcset="
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w165h90/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-024-53387-y/MediaObjects/41467_2024_53387_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 160w,
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-024-53387-y/MediaObjects/41467_2024_53387_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 290w" type="image/webp">
                 <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41467-024-53387-y/MediaObjects/41467_2024_53387_Fig1_HTML.png"/>
                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41467-024-53387-y" itemprop="url">
                 LLM-driven multimodal target volume contouring in radiation oncology
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 The integration of multimodal knowledge would be essential for radiation oncologist to determine the therapeutic treatment. Here, inspired by the large language models facilitating the integration of textural information and images, this group reports a 3D multimodal clinical target volume delineation model combining image and text-based clinical information for decision-making in radiation oncology.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">

                 LLM-based agentic systems in medicine and healthcare
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Large language model-based agentic systems can process input information, plan and decide, recall and reflect, interact and collaborate, leverage various tools and act. This opens up a wealth of opportunities within medicine and healthcare, ranging from clinical workflow automation to multi-agent-aided diagnosis.
                </p>

               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s42256-025-00986-z" itemprop="url">
                 Large language models that replace human participants can harmfully misportray and flatten identity groups
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Large language models are being considered to simulate responses from participants of different backgrounds in computational social science experiments. Here it is shown that this practice can misportray and flatten demographic groups in distinctively harmful ways.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact" data-test="author-list">

                 Integrated image-based deep learning and language models for primary diabetes care
                </a>

           <div class="u-full-height" data-native-ad-placement="false">
            <article class="u-full-height c-card c-card--flush" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ScholarlyArticle">
             <div class="c-card__layout u-full-height">
              <div class="c-card__image">
               <picture>
                <source sizes="
                                    (max-width: 640px) 160px,
                                    (max-width: 1200px) 290px,
                                    290px" srcset="
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w165h90/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41591-024-03456-y/MediaObjects/41591_2024_3456_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 160w,
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41591-024-03456-y/MediaObjects/41591_2024_3456_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 290w" type="image/webp">
                 <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41591-024-03456-y/MediaObjects/41591_2024_3456_Fig1_HTML.png"/>
                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41591-024-03456-y" itemprop="url">
                 GPT-4 assistance for improvement of physician performance on patient care tasks: a randomized controlled trial
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 In a prospective study involving 92 physicians from multiple institutions, access to large language model assistance on top of conventional resources increased a score expressing the quality of their reasoning in addressing patient care while assessing five clinical vignettes.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Ethan Goh

               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s42256-025-00985-0" itemprop="url">
                 Rethinking machine unlearning for large language models
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Machine unlearning techniques remove undesirable data and associated model capabilities while preserving essential knowledge, so that machine learning models can be updated without costly retraining. Liu et al. review recent advances and opportunities in machine unlearning in LLMs, revisiting methodologies and overlooked principles for future improvements and exploring emerging applications in copyright and privacy safeguards and in reducing sociotechnical harms.
                </p>
               </div>

                </a>

                 Medical large language models are vulnerable to data-poisoning attacks
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Large language models can be manipulated to generate misinformation by poisoning of a very small percentage of the data on which they are trained, but a harm mitigation strategy using biomedical knowledge graphs can offer a method for addressing this vulnerability.
                </p>

                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">

              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41592-024-02525-x" itemprop="url">
                 Evaluation of large language models for discovery of gene set function
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Large language models show potential in suggesting common functions for a gene set.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">

              <span class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="article.type">

               </span>

              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg u-text-bold" data-test="journal-title-and-link">

              </div>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="volume-and-page-info">

              </div>

         <li class="app-article-list-row__item">
          <div class="u-full-height">
           <div class="u-full-height" data-native-ad-placement="false">
            <article class="u-full-height c-card c-card--flush" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ScholarlyArticle">
             <div class="c-card__layout u-full-height">
              <div class="c-card__image">
               <picture>
                <source sizes="
                                    (max-width: 640px) 160px,
                                    (max-width: 1200px) 290px,
                                    290px" srcset="
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w165h90/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-024-00925-4/MediaObjects/42256_2024_925_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 160w,
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-024-00925-4/MediaObjects/42256_2024_925_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 290w" type="image/webp">
                 <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-024-00925-4/MediaObjects/42256_2024_925_Fig1_HTML.png"/>
                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s42256-024-00925-4" itemprop="url">
                 Contextual feature extraction hierarchies converge in large language models and the brain
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Why brain-like feature extraction emerges in large language models (LLMs) remains elusive. Mischler, Li and colleagues demonstrate that high-performing LLMs not only predict neural responses more accurately than other LLMs but also align more closely with the hierarchical language processing pathway in the brain, revealing parallels between these models and human cognitive mechanisms.
                </p>
               </div>

               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41578-025-00772-8" itemprop="url">
                 Large language models for reticular chemistry
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Large language models can accelerate reticular chemistry by guiding material design, data interpretation and discovery. This Perspective discusses how large language models integrate into laboratory workflows and modular artificial intelligence systems, streamlining data-driven research for new materials and tackling crystallization challenges.
                </p>

             <div class="c-card__layout u-full-height">
              <div class="c-card__image">
               <picture>
                <source sizes="
                                    (max-width: 640px) 160px,
                                    (max-width: 1200px) 290px,
                                    290px" srcset="
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w165h90/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs43588-025-00768-y/MediaObjects/43588_2025_768_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 160w,
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs43588-025-00768-y/MediaObjects/43588_2025_768_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 290w" type="image/webp">
                 <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs43588-025-00768-y/MediaObjects/43588_2025_768_Fig1_HTML.png"/>
                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s43588-025-00768-y" itemprop="url">
                 Harnessing large language models for data-scarce learning of polymer properties
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 A physics-based training pipeline is developed to help tackle the challenges of data scarcity. The framework aligns large language models to a physically consistent initial state that is fine-tuned for learning polymer properties.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Ning Liu
                 </span>
                </li>
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Siavash Jafarzadeh
                 </span>
                </li>
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Yue Yu
                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>

                 Learning and actioning general principles of cancer cell drug sensitivity
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Potential anti-tumor therapies remain to be discovered in cancer cell line high-throughput screening datasets. Here, the authors develop a machine learning approach to infer cancer cell drug sensitivity from transcriptomics data and to explore drug mechanisms of action, and predict effective drugs for pancreatic cancer and glioblastoma.

                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Large language models (LLMs) can synthesize vast amounts of information. Luo et al. show that LLMs—especially BrainGPT, an LLM the authors tuned on the neuroscience literature—outperform experts in predicting neuroscience results and could assist scientists in making future discoveries.
                </p>

                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>

               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41586-024-08025-4" itemprop="url">
                 Scalable watermarking for identifying large language model outputs
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 A scheme for watermarking the text generated by large language models shows high text quality preservation and detection accuracy and low latency, and is feasible in large-scale-production settings.
                </p>
               </div>

                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s41598-024-53255-1" itemprop="url">
                 A pilot study of measuring emotional response and perception of LLM-generated questionnaire and human-generated questionnaires
                </a>
               </h3>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">

                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Luqman Ali
                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="c-card__section c-meta">
              <span class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="article.type">

                Research

              <time class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" datetime="2024-02-02" itemprop="datePublished">
               02 Feb 2024
              </time>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg u-text-bold" data-test="journal-title-and-link">
               Scientific Reports
              </div>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="volume-and-page-info">

              </div>

          <div class="u-full-height">
           <div class="u-full-height" data-native-ad-placement="false">
            <article class="u-full-height c-card c-card--flush" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ScholarlyArticle">
             <div class="c-card__layout u-full-height">
              <div class="c-card__image">
               <picture>
                <source sizes="
                                    (max-width: 640px) 160px,
                                    (max-width: 1200px) 290px,
                                    290px" srcset="
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w165h90/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-025-01013-x/MediaObjects/42256_2025_1013_Figa_HTML.png?as=webp 160w,
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-025-01013-x/MediaObjects/42256_2025_1013_Figa_HTML.png?as=webp 290w" type="image/webp">
                 <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-025-01013-x/MediaObjects/42256_2025_1013_Figa_HTML.png"/>
                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s42256-025-01013-x" itemprop="url">
                 Bridging the gap between machine confidence and human perceptions
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Users often overestimate the accuracy of large language models (LLMs). A new approach examines user perceptions and finds that aligning LLM explanations with the models’ internal confidence improves user perception.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact" data-test="author-list">
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Ming Yin
                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="c-card__section c-meta">
              <span class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="article.type">
               <span class="c-meta__type">
                News &amp; Views
               </span>
              </span>
              <time class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" datetime="2025-03-03" itemprop="datePublished">
               03 Mar 2025
              </time>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg u-text-bold" data-test="journal-title-and-link">
               Nature Machine Intelligence
              </div>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="volume-and-page-info">
               P: 1-2
              </div>
             </div>
            </article>
           </div>
          </div>
         </li>
         <li class="app-article-list-row__item">
          <div class="u-full-height">
           <div class="u-full-height" data-native-ad-placement="false">
            <article class="u-full-height c-card c-card--flush" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ScholarlyArticle">
             <div class="c-card__layout u-full-height">
              <div class="c-card__image">
               <picture>
                <source sizes="
                                    (max-width: 640px) 160px,
                                    (max-width: 1200px) 290px,
                                    290px" srcset="
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w165h90/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-025-00994-z/MediaObjects/42256_2025_994_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 160w,
                                    https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-025-00994-z/MediaObjects/42256_2025_994_Fig1_HTML.png?as=webp 290w" type="image/webp">
                 <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="https://media.springernature.com/w290h158/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1038%2Fs42256-025-00994-z/MediaObjects/42256_2025_994_Fig1_HTML.png"/>
                </source>
               </picture>
              </div>
              <div class="c-card__body u-display-flex u-flex-direction-column">
               <h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a class="c-card__link u-link-inherit" data-track="click" data-track-action="view article" data-track-label="link" href="/articles/s42256-025-00994-z" itemprop="url">
                 Large language models for scientific discovery in molecular property prediction
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="c-card__summary u-mb-16 u-hide-sm-max" data-test="article-description" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 Zheng et al. developed LLM4SD, a framework using large language models to predict molecular properties. The method leverages the ability of large language models to synthesize knowledge from literature and to reason about scientific data with domain expertise.
                </p>
               </div>
               <ul class="c-author-list c-author-list--compact c-author-list--truncated" data-test="author-list">
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Yizhen Zheng
                 </span>
                </li>
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Huan Yee Koh
                 </span>
                </li>
                <li itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                 <span itemprop="name">
                  Shirui Pan
                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="c-card__section c-meta">
              <span class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="article.type">
               <span class="c-meta__type">
                Research
               </span>
              </span>
              <time class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" datetime="2025-02-25" itemprop="datePublished">
               25 Feb 2025
              </time>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg u-text-bold" data-test="journal-title-and-link">
               Nature Machine Intelligence
              </div>
              <div class="c-meta__item c-meta__item--block-at-lg" data-test="volume-and-page-info">
               P: 1-11
              </div>
             </div>
            </article>
           </div>
